### Abbreviating de Bruijn indices

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Problem2.lookup"></a><a id="2595" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#2595" class="Function">lookup</a> <a id="2602" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2604" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#1610" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="2612" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2614" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#97" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="2616" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2618" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#1537" class="Datatype">Type</a>

  <a id="6537" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#6463" class="Function Operator">begin</a> <a id="6543" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#6543" class="Bound">M—↠N</a> <a id="6548" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6550" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#6543" class="Bound">M—↠N</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### Type equality

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Problem3._≟Tp_"></a><a id="11009" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#11009" class="Function Operator">_≟Tp_</a> <a id="11015" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11017" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11018" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#11018" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="11020" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#11020" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="11022" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11024" href="plfa.DeBruijn.html#8177" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="11028" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11030" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11032" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#534" class="Datatype">Dec</a> <a id="11036" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11037" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#11018" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="11039" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="11041" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#11020" class="Bound">B</a><a id="11042" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="11046" href="plfa.DeBruijn.html#8223" class="InductiveConstructor">`ℕ</a>      <a id="11054" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#11009" class="Function Operator">≟Tp</a> <a id="11058" href="plfa.DeBruijn.html#8223" class="InductiveConstructor">`ℕ</a>              <a id="11074" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="11077" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#570" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="11081" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>

### Promoting negations
